         <h1 class="entry-title"><a href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/" rel="bookmark">How to Send e-mail using Node.js</a></h1> 
         <ul class="social-share"> 
          <li> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/" title="Share on Facebook" target="_blank" onclick="window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=' + encodeURIComponent(document.URL) + '&amp;t=' + encodeURIComponent(document.URL)); return false;" class="ss-facebook"><span>Share on Facebook</span></a> </li> 
          <li> <a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?source=https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/&amp;text=How to Send e-mail using Node.js" target="_blank" title="Tweet" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=' + encodeURIComponent(document.title) + ':%20'  + encodeURIComponent(document.URL)); return false;" class="ss-twitter"><span>Tweet This</span></a> </li> 
          <li> <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/" target="_blank" title="Share on Google+" onclick="window.open('https://plus.google.com/share?url=' + encodeURIComponent(document.URL)); return false;" class="ss-googleplus"><span>Share on Google+</span></a> </li> 
          <li> <a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/&amp;description=How to Send e-mail using Node.js" target="_blank" title="Pin it" onclick="window.open('http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=' + encodeURIComponent(document.URL) + '&amp;description=' +  encodeURIComponent(document.title)); return false;" class="ss-pinterest"><span>Pin This</span></a> </li>

         <div class="entry-meta"> 
          <ul class="em-list tbl"> 
           <li class="em-photo"> </li> 
           <li> <label>Author</label> <p><span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://codeforgeek.com/author/shahid/">Shahid (UnixRoot) Shaikh</a></span></p> </li> 
           <li> <label>Last Edited</label> <p><a href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/" rel="bookmark"><time class="entry-date published" datetime="2014-07-14T15:28:50+00:00">Jul 14, 2014</time></a></p> </li> 
           <li> <label>Comments</label> <p>147</p> </li> 
          </ul> 
         </div> 
        </header> 
        <div class="entry-content"> 
         <p>In this tutorial i am going to discuss about sending e-mail with Node.js. I have already covered Express.js tutorials and in this tutorial also i am going to use Express.js and <strong>NodeMailer</strong> package. In many forums and blogs people used to ask about sending e-mails using Node.js for account verification, password recovery and promotion. So lets begin with tutorial and at the end you will have Node application which is able to send e-mails to any ones account.</p> 
         <blockquote>

         <h2>What we are Building ?</h2> 
         <p><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-106" src="https://i1.wp.com/104.131.231.142/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/mailer.png?resize=640%2C326" alt="How to send e-mail in node.js" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/codeforgeek.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/mailer.png?w=700&amp;ssl=1 700w, https://i2.wp.com/codeforgeek.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/mailer.png?resize=300%2C153&amp;ssl=1 300w" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> 
         <p>Create <strong>package.json </strong>file and keep it in any folder. Put the below code in it.</p> 
         <div class="file_name">
          <strong>package.json</strong>
         </div> 
         <div class="codecolorer-container text twitlight" style="overflow:auto;white-space:nowrap;width:99%;">
          <div class="text codecolorer">
           {
           <br> &nbsp; "name": "email-node",
           <br> &nbsp; "version": "1.0.0",
           <br> &nbsp; "dependencies": {
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; "nodemailer": "latest",
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; "express": "latest"
           <br> &nbsp; }
           <br> }
          </div>
         </div> 
         <p>Once done. Switch to that folder using Command prompt or Terminal and type <strong>npm install. </strong>It will download and install the dependencies our project need. After completion you will able to see <strong>node_modules </strong>folder in your project directory.</p>

         <h2>Adding NodeMailer code:</h2> 
         <p>Okay we are almost there, now we have to handle the Mail system. First of all we have to Define Mail transport System (SMTP) so that from that E-mail box our e-mail will be sent. For ease, you can add your Gmail account and password. Add this code just in <b>Server.js</b> just below the var app=express() line.</p> 
         <div class="codecolorer-container javascript twitlight" style="overflow:auto;white-space:nowrap;width:99%;">
          <div class="javascript codecolorer">
           <span class="kw1">var</span> smtpTransport 
           <span class="sy0">=</span> nodemailer.
           <span class="me1">createTransport</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; service
           <span class="sy0">:</span> 
           <span class="st0">"gmail"</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; host
           <span class="sy0">:</span> 
           <span class="st0">"smtp.gmail.com"</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; auth
           <span class="sy0">:</span> 
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; user
           <span class="sy0">:</span> 
           <span class="st0">""</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; pass
           <span class="sy0">:</span> 
           <span class="st0">""</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
          </div>
         </div> 
         <p>We will use this Object to send e-mail. Our app design is when user click on Send email Button then only e-mail should be sent, and we have did that part in <b>app.get(/send)</b> router. So in that block only paste the code shown below.</p>

           <br>

           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="br0">}</span>

          <strong>Server.js</strong>
         </div> 
         <div class="codecolorer-container javascript twitlight" style="overflow:auto;white-space:nowrap;width:99%;">

           <span class="kw1">var</span> express
           <span class="sy0">=</span>require
           <span class="br0">(</span>

           <span class="sy0">=</span> nodemailer.

           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; user
           <span class="sy0">:</span>

           <span class="sy0">,</span>

           <br> 
           <br> app.
           <span class="kw1">get</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">'/'</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <span class="kw1">function</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>req
           <span class="sy0">,</span>res
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; res.
           <span class="me1">sendfile</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">'index.html'</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> app.
           <span class="kw1">get</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">'/send'</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <span class="kw1">function</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>req
           <span class="sy0">,</span>res
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; 
           <span class="kw1">var</span> mailOptions
           <span class="sy0">=</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; to 
           <span class="sy0">:</span> req.
           <span class="me1">query</span>.
           <span class="me1">to</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; subject 
           <span class="sy0">:</span> req.
           <span class="me1">query</span>.
           <span class="me1">subject</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; text 
           <span class="sy0">:</span> req.
           <span class="me1">query</span>.
           <span class="me1">text</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; console.
           <span class="me1">log</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>mailOptions
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; smtpTransport.
           <span class="me1">sendMail</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>mailOptions
           <span class="sy0">,</span> 
           <span class="kw1">function</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>error
           <span class="sy0">,</span> response
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
           <span class="kw1">if</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>error
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; console.
           <span class="me1">log</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>error
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; res.
           <span class="me1">end</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">"error"</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <span class="kw1">else</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; console.
           <span class="me1">log</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">"Message sent: "</span> 
           <span class="sy0">+</span> response.
           <span class="me1">message</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; res.
           <span class="me1">end</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">"sent"</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> 
           <br> 
           <span class="coMULTI">/*--------------------Routing Over----------------------------*/</span>
           <br> 
           <br> app.
           <span class="me1">listen</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="nu0">3000</span>
           <span class="sy0">,</span>
           <span class="kw1">function</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="br0">{</span>
           <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; console.
           <span class="me1">log</span>
           <span class="br0">(</span>
           <span class="st0">"Express Started on Port 3000"</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="br0">}</span>
           <span class="br0">)</span>
           <span class="sy0">;</span>

           <span class="sc-2">$(document).ready(function(){</span>

           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; $("#send_email").click(function(){&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; </span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; to=$("#to").val();</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; subject=$("#subject").val();</span>

           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; text=$("#content").val();</span>

           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; $.get("http://localhost:3000/send",{to:to,subject:subject,text:text},function(data){</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if(data=="sent")</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; {</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; $("#message").empty().html("</span>
           <br> 
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">Email is been sent at "+to+" . Please check inbox!</span>
           <br> 
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">");</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</span>
           <br> 
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">});</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">&nbsp; &nbsp; });</span>
           <br> 
           <span class="sc-2">});</span>

           <div class="comment-content"> 
            <p>Hello Shahid,</p> 
            <p>On my website Im working on implementing the contact form. Im trying to modularize my mailer. I put the var smtpTransport in the server.js</p> 
            <p>I know my routes are connect because I tell my server to use the routes file. I used your routes code as so:</p> 
            <p>// Code for mailer functionality<br> app.get(/, function(request, response){<br> response.sendfile(index.html);<br> });</p> 
            <p> app.post(/, function(request, response){<br> console.log(in mail controller);<br> var mailOptions = {<br> to: request.body.contact_email,<br> subject: request.body.subject,<br> text: request.body.message<br> }<br> console.log(mailOptions);<br> smtpTransport.sendMail(mailOptions, function(error, response){<br> if (error) {<br> console.log(error);<br> response.end(error);<br> } else {<br> console.log(Message sent:  + response.message);<br> response.end(sent);<br> }<br> })<br> });</p> 
            <p>So i know that the send button is accessing this controller because my console says in mailer controller, however my errors are as followed:</p> 
            <p>{ to: undefined, subject: undefined, text: undefined }<br> ReferenceError: smtpTransport is not defined</p> 
            <p>Im pretty sure once I get the smtpTransport defined in my server that it will work, however I thought that because the route file talks to the server js that I should be able to call a global variable defined in my server.js file, but I must be mistaken. Can you lead me in the right direction here?</p> 
            <p>Many Thanks!<br> Im also searching google for the answer, but supposed other beginner viewers would find this question helpful as well.</p>

             <footer class="comment-meta"> 
              <div class="comment-author vcard"> 
               <img alt="" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c178ed2e3974874e691d8041c6480781?s=150&amp;d=https%3A%2F%2Fcodeforgeek.com%2Fwp-content%2Fthemes%2Fcodeforgeek%2Fimg%2Fauthor-placeholder.png&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c178ed2e3974874e691d8041c6480781?s=300&amp;d=https%3A%2F%2Fcodeforgeek.com%2Fwp-content%2Fthemes%2Fcodeforgeek%2Fimg%2Fauthor-placeholder.png&amp;r=g 2x" class="avatar avatar-150 photo" height="150" width="150"> 
               <b class="fn"><a href="http://www.codeforgeek.com" rel="external nofollow" class="url">Shahid Shaikh</a></b> 
               <span class="says">says:</span> 
              </div> 
              <div class="comment-metadata"> 
               <a href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/#comment-28"> <time datetime="2015-01-11T01:24:37+00:00"> Jan 11, 2015 at 1:24 am </time> </a> 
              </div> 
             </footer> 
             <div class="comment-content"> 
              <p>Make sure you define smtpTransport above the routes in server.js and pass it to route file. assuming server.js contains smtpTransport variable and route.js contains router, so when you define route in server like this.</p> 
              <p>var route = require(route) //point to route.js</p> 
              <p>do it like this instead.</p> 
              <p>var route = require(route)(smtpTransport) </p> 
              <p>Give it a shot !</p> 
             </div>

             <li id="comment-33" class="comment even depth-3 parent"> 
              <article id="div-comment-33" class="comment-body"> 
               <footer class="comment-meta"> 
                <div class="comment-author vcard"> 
                 <img alt="" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1828490c74a7f949e13cdf476c1da682?s=150&amp;d=https%3A%2F%2Fcodeforgeek.com%2Fwp-content%2Fthemes%2Fcodeforgeek%2Fimg%2Fauthor-placeholder.png&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/1828490c74a7f949e13cdf476c1da682?s=300&amp;d=https%3A%2F%2Fcodeforgeek.com%2Fwp-content%2Fthemes%2Fcodeforgeek%2Fimg%2Fauthor-placeholder.png&amp;r=g 2x" class="avatar avatar-150 photo" height="150" width="150"> 
                 <b class="fn"><a href="http://www.ashupradhan.cu.cc" rel="external nofollow" class="url">Ashutosh Pradhan</a></b> 
                 <span class="says">says:</span> 
                </div> 
                <div class="comment-metadata"> 
                 <a href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/#comment-33"> <time datetime="2015-02-10T11:18:47+00:00"> Feb 10, 2015 at 11:18 am </time> </a> 
                </div> 
               </footer> 
               <div class="comment-content"> 
                <p>$scope.sendmail = function () {<br> var dataToPost = {to: <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="e8899b809d898680898ca88f85898184c68b8785">[email&nbsp;protected]</a>}; /* PostData*/<br> $http.get(/send, dataToPost)<br> .success(function(serverResponse) {</p> 
                <p> console.log(serverResponse);<br> }).error(function(serverResponse) {<br> console.log(serverResponse);<br> });<br> };</p> 
                <p>this is my client side script to send the email field to server.<br> server code is same as yours but it is not sending mail to the email address.</p> 
               </div> 
               <div class="reply">
                <a rel="nofollow" class="comment-reply-link" href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/?replytocom=33#respond" onclick="return addComment.moveForm( &quot;div-comment-33&quot;, &quot;33&quot;, &quot;respond&quot;, &quot;105&quot; )" aria-label="Reply to Ashutosh Pradhan">Reply</a>

                     <b class="fn"><a href="http://www.codeforgeek.com" rel="external nofollow" class="url">Shahid Shaikh</a></b> 
                     <span class="says">says:</span> 
                    </div> 
                    <div class="comment-metadata"> 
                     <a href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/#comment-50"> <time datetime="2015-03-04T12:14:58+00:00"> Mar 4, 2015 at 12:14 pm </time> </a> 
                    </div> 
                   </footer> 
                   <div class="comment-content"> 
                    <p>Like i told you its happening because of callback nature of Node.js Member.find is executing and while its execution Node.js is executing next statement which is console.log(self.membercount);. What you need to make sure is when members.find finish its execution then update the flag to true and access the console.log(self.membercount);. This way execution will halt until and unless members.find() finish its execution.</p> 
                   </div>

           <div class="comment-content"> 
            <p>Hi there,</p> 
            <p>First off, this is an awesome tutorial. Im trying to implement a contact form similar to this on my porfolio page, but when I press send, on the console I get </p> 
            <p>Cross-Origin Request Blocked: The Same Origin Policy disallows reading the remote resource at <a href="http://muhsinking.com:3000/send?to=muhsinking%40gmail.com&amp;subject=example+name&amp;text=example+message" rel="nofollow">http://muhsinking.com:3000/send?to=muhsinking%40gmail.com&amp;subject=example+name&amp;text=example+message</a>.            <li id="comment-79" class="comment byuser comment-author-shahid bypostauthor odd alt depth-2"> 
            <article id="div-comment-79" class="comment-body"> 
             <footer class="comment-meta"> 
              <div class="comment-author vcard"> 
               <img alt="" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c178ed2e3974874e691d8041c6480781?s=150&amp;d=https%3A%2F%2Fcodeforgeek.com%2Fwp-content%2Fthemes%2Fcodeforgeek%2Fimg%2Fauthor-placeholder.png&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/c178ed2e3974874e691d8041c6480781?s=300&amp;d=https%3A%2F%2Fcodeforgeek.com%2Fwp-content%2Fthemes%2Fcodeforgeek%2Fimg%2Fauthor-placeholder.png&amp;r=g 2x" class="avatar avatar-150 photo" height="150" width="150"> 
               <b class="fn"><a href="http://www.codeforgeek.com" rel="external nofollow" class="url">Shahid Shaikh</a></b> 
               <span class="says">says:</span> 
              </div> 
              <div class="comment-metadata"> 
               <a href="https://codeforgeek.com/2014/07/send-e-mail-node-js/#comment-79"> <time datetime="2015-06-30T09:58:36+00:00"> Jun 30, 2015 at 9:58 am </time> </a> 
              </div> 
             </footer> 
             <div class="comment-content"> 
              <p>Yes try allowing cross origin request in node server. Here is code.</p> 
              <div class="codecolorer-container javascript twitlight" style="overflow:auto;white-space:nowrap;width:99%;">
               <div class="javascript codecolorer">
                app.
                <span class="me1">use</span>
                <span class="br0">(</span>
                <span class="st0">'*'</span>
                <span class="sy0">,</span> 
                <span class="kw1">function</span>
                <span class="br0">(</span>req
                <span class="sy0">,</span> res
                <span class="sy0">,</span> next
                <span class="br0">)</span> 
                <span class="br0">{</span>
                <br> &nbsp; res.
                <span class="me1">header</span>
                <span class="br0">(</span>
                <span class="st0">"Access-Control-Allow-Origin"</span>
                <span class="sy0">,</span> 
                <span class="st0">"*"</span>
                <span class="br0">)</span>
                <span class="sy0">;</span>
                <br> &nbsp; res.
                <span class="me1">header</span>
                <span class="br0">(</span>
                <span class="st0">"Access-Control-Allow-Headers"</span>
                <span class="sy0">,</span> 
                <span class="st0">"X-Requested-With"</span>
                <span class="br0">)</span>
                <span class="sy0">;</span>
                <br> &nbsp; next
                <span class="br0">(</span>
                <span class="br0">)</span>
                <span class="sy0">;</span>
                <br> &nbsp;
                <span class="br0">}</span>
                <span class="br0">)</span>
                <span class="sy0">;</span>
               </div>
              </div> 
              <p>Paste it on start of router.</p> 
             </div>

              <span class="br0">{</span> title
              <span class="sy0">:</span> 
              <span class="st0">'Raging Flame Laboratory - Contact'</span>
              <span class="sy0">,</span> msg
              <span class="sy0">:</span> 
              <span class="st0">'Error occured, message not sent.'</span>
              <span class="sy0">,</span> err
              <span class="sy0">:</span> 
              <span class="kw2">true</span>
              <span class="sy0">,</span> page
              <span class="sy0">:</span> 
              <span class="st0">'contact'</span> 
              <span class="br0">}</span>
              <span class="br0">)</span>
              <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 
              <span class="br0">}</span>
              <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 
              <span class="co1">//Yay!! Email sent</span>
              <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; 
              <span class="kw1">else</span> 
              <span class="br0">{</span>
              <br> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; res.
              <span class="me1">render</span>
              <span class="br0">(</span>
              <span class="st0">'contact'</span>
              <span class="sy0">,</span> 
              <span class="br0">{</span> title
              <span class="sy0">:</span> 
              <span class="st0">'Raging Flame Laboratory - Contact'</span>

              <span class="br0">)</span>

           <div class="comment-content"> 
            <p>In my case problem was in following code:<br> var smtpTransport = nodemailer.createTransport(SMTP,{<br> service: Gmail,<br> auth: {<br> user: <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="accdcecfeccdcecf82cfc3c1">[email&nbsp;protected]</a>,<br> pass: ********<br> }<br> });</p> 
            <p>I removed SMTP and now, it is working fine.</p>
